Product Catalog

Welded Steel Tubing

Steel Tubing Product Catalog


Valmont Tubing manufactures one of the broadest size ranges of welded mechanical steel tubing in the industry with the type, shape, and size of product made to your precise specifications. Valmont Tubing's frequent roll cycles, lower mill minimums and focus on customer needs, means that your tubing order is delivered on time and as ordered.  For all of your large OD, light wall electric resistance welded tubing, Valmont Tubing is the producer of choice.

Please review our on-line steel tubing product catalog below that provides you with specific information concerning our capabilities.  By searching on the shape, size and/or finish, you will find the available wall thicknesses, ASTM specifications and weight per foot information for your selection.  We encourage you to bookmark this page for future reference. For pricing & delivery information on any of these sizes listed or for more information on a size or special shape not listed below, please call us at 1-800-825-6668 or email us at tubing@valmont.com.  We want to hear from you!
